8Back in 1997 a brazilian kid by the alias of enzo pops up out of nowhere15 8and    
8starts rawing ansi, not much longer after he was known as the goto guy for toon 
8style pieces.. there was alot of toonage back then, but through it all enzo     
8stood out from the rest.. Here is his earlier work in Maiden brazil.. not to be 
8mixed up with black maiden..                                                    
8So as you can see, this is very early enzo stuff, but he learn't quick, i think 
8you had to back then, the scene was very.. VERY competitive and well, lets see  
8the evolutionary steps of enzo.                                                 
8His ansis started taking shape, notably his toons tended to have one eye bigger 
8than the other, and when he started becoming more comfortable with the medium   
8i think his personality/creativity started to show more..                       
8After becoming known as the toon master i think his skills took a turn for the  
8better.. he started looking outside the realm of toon and started looking at    
8various styles and started applying them to his newer works.. being smallscale  
8originals, or large scale comic rips.. he could do it all, and i think the style
8of shading he had separated him from alot of other people at the time.          
8Also, the fact that he did alot of toon work when he started enabled him to     
8draw crazy ass originals later on in his works.                                 
8The guy was versatile as anything, having joined groups such as maiden brazil,  
8echo, glue, ice and founding 27inch, and blocktronics he learned alot from      
8other artists and just got better and better over time. Innovator yes..         
8definitely, one of a kind.
